<div class="gb-container gb-container-d7474131">
<div class="gb-container gb-container-60a43fda">

<h1 class="gb-headline gb-headline-84b2a9b5 gb-headline-text">Watchmaking Tools for Watchmakers</h1>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-b7825818 gb-headline-text">What began as a small intrigue in horology led to the birth of the WatchmakingTools website, a global platform helping you navigate the labyrinth of mechanical watch servicing and repair.  WatchmakingTools is your ultimate watchmaking resources center, an online toolbox with all the tips, tricks, and education you need to learn watchmaking.</p>

</div>
</div>

<div class="gb-container gb-container-001c1df5">
<div class="gb-container gb-container-cd1a76c5">
<div class="gb-grid-wrapper gb-grid-wrapper-ca123371">
<div class="gb-grid-column gb-grid-column-9e5b3c45"><div class="gb-container gb-container-9e5b3c45">
<div class="gb-container gb-container-105e285a">

<h3 class="gb-headline gb-headline-a1620213 gb-headline-text">Co-founded by Watch Enthusiast Maz</h3>


<div class="gb-container gb-container-5c8417a1">

<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-a5b90f0b gb-headline-text">WatchmakingTools is ever-evolving with a collection of watchmaker resources, guides, and <a class="wpil_keyword_link" href="https://watchmakingtools.com/facts-about-patek-philippe-watches/" title="Masterpieces of Craftsmanship: Unraveling the Facts About Patek Philippe Watches" data-wpil-keyword-link="linked" data-wpil-monitor-id="244" data-lasso-id="17888">blog</a> posts that are constantly expanding.  Always interested in mechanical movements, Maz started with a small collection of <strong><a href="https://watchmakingtools.com/swatch-battery-replacement/" data-type="post" data-id="5924" data-lasso-id="12375">Swatch watches</a> </strong>and <a data-lasso-id="133" href="https://watchmakingtools.com/movements/seiko/" data-type="page" data-id="1312"><strong>vintage Seiko chronographs</strong></a> before creating WatchmakingTools. </p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-55455e45 gb-headline-text">In 2019, he decided to take his passion to the next level, taking the plunge to sign up for an extensive 40-week beginners <a class="wpil_keyword_link" href="https://watchmakingtools.com/watchmaking-resources/new-to-watchmaking/" title="New to Watchmaking" data-wpil-keyword-link="linked" data-wpil-monitor-id="2803" data-lasso-id="20289">watchmaking</a> course.  Studying the year-long Introduction to Mechanical Watchmaking course at <a href="https://efhc.org.uk/wordpress/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-lasso-id="16841"><strong>Epping Forest Horology Centre</strong></a> was quite the journey.  </p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-9a818a1d gb-headline-text">During the course, in-person classes transformed into online during lockdown and whilst this was an initial challenge, the events of 2020 did not deter Maz who then signed up for the following year’s course.  The rest, as they say, is history.</p>

</div>

<div class="gb-container gb-container-e110ddac">

<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-7fafc604 gb-headline-text">In the early years of his <a class="wpil_keyword_link" href="https://watchmakingtools.com/movements/seiko/seiko-oiling-points/seiko-2565-oiling-points/" title="Seiko 2565 Oiling Points &#8211; Watch Lubrication Guide" data-wpil-keyword-link="linked" data-wpil-monitor-id="64992" data-lasso-id="1935700">watchmaking journey</a>, Maz encountered difficulty finding resources online within this niche area.  As a topic that is not mainstream, information on watchmaking is difficult to wade through and Maz found himself spending endless hours searching for answers to his questions and queries.  </p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-5f9962b9 gb-headline-text">This frustration sparked the idea for WatchmakingTools.  Not only was WatchmakingTools built to share Maz’s passion for watchmaking, but it was also created to help you find the essential information that you need on your watchmaking journey.</p>

</div>

<div class="gb-container gb-container-7bfd4fb7">

<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-2d437f7d gb-headline-text">If you are in search of <a href="https://watchmakingtools.com/watchmaking-resources/blog/" data-type="page" data-id="13937" data-lasso-id="16930"><strong>watchmaking tips</strong></a> and the tools you&#8217;ll need to help you improve your watchmaking skills, you have come to the right place.  WatchmakingTools is an outstanding resource in the world of horology, with advice and guidance from someone who has been in your exact position in the watchmaking process. </p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-22293aa8 gb-headline-text">Here at WatchmakingTools, you will find an extensive selection of tips, posts, and reviews on all things watchmaking.  WatchmakingTools brings this time-old tradition into the digital age with an impressive collection of guides and resources available online and all in one place.  No more scouring the internet to pinpoint your issue, your answers lie here at WatchmakingTools.</p>


<div class="gb-container gb-container-8b75459f">

<a class="gb-button gb-button-3512e50b" href="https://watchmakingtools.com/about/" data-lasso-id="7286"><span class="gb-button-text">learn more about us</span><span class="gb-icon"><svg viewbox="0 0 256 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M224.3 273l-136 136c-9.4 9.4-24.6 9.4-33.9 0l-22.6-22.6c-9.4-9.4-9.4-24.6 0-33.9l96.4-96.4-96.4-96.4c-9.4-9.4-9.4-24.6 0-33.9L54.3 103c9.4-9.4 24.6-9.4 33.9 0l136 136c9.5 9.4 9.5 24.6.1 34z"></path></svg></span></a>

<h2 class="gb-headline gb-headline-16dccc24 gb-headline-text">What Can I Find on the WatchmakingTools Website?</h2>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-cdf461e3 gb-headline-text">WatchmakingTools is your ultimate resource in the <a data-wpil-monitor-id="9" data-lasso-id="15306" href="https://watchmakingtools.com/watchmaking-resources/watchmaking-history/"><strong>history of watchmaking</strong></a> and the watch industry.  Here you will find advice and guidance from a passionate watchmaker who is on the exact same journey as you are.  Enter the world of horological craftsmanship and embark on your watchmaking adventure with all the educational insight you need as a beginner.  </p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-9b50f995 gb-headline-text">Discover honest and detailed reviews on the essential <a class="wpil_keyword_link" href="https://watchmakingtools.com/tools/watchmakers-tools/" title="Watchmakers Tools" data-wpil-keyword-link="linked" data-wpil-monitor-id="7318" data-lasso-id="24498">watchmaking tools</a> that you can buy to enhance and assist your watchmaking as well as handy tips on household products that can be repurposed into affordable watchmaking tools.  Explore the <a data-lasso-id="4869" href="https://watchmakingtools.com/watchmaking-resources/" data-type="page" data-id="374"><strong>Watchmaking Resources</strong></a> section to find key information about specific <strong><a data-lasso-id="4870" href="https://watchmakingtools.com/movements/" data-type="page" data-id="434">watch movements</a></strong>.  For everything watchmaking, find it here at WatchmakingTools.</p>

<div class="gb-grid-column gb-grid-column-76f71ce7"><div class="gb-container gb-container-76f71ce7">
<div class="gb-container gb-container-6aadd635">

<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-126255cc gb-headline-text">If this is your first step into watches in general, welcome.  The watchmaking community is one of incredible skill, extensive knowledge, and extraordinary attention to detail so rest assured that you are in safe hands.</p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-c112837a gb-headline-text">If you have always been intrigued by <strong><a href="https://watchmakingtools.com/watchmaking-resources/watch-terminology/#Horology" data-type="link" data-id="http://watchmakingtools.com/watchmaking-resources/watch-terminology/#Horology" data-lasso-id="12393">horology</a></strong> and are growing your pocket watch or wristwatch collection, watchmaking is an excellent way to expand and grow your passion.</p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-54a8bd24 gb-headline-text">Watchmaking is an art form, the ultimate hobby for someone with a fascination with horology. It requires time, commitment, and patience, a passion that should be pursued as a mild obsession.</p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-bc8f908a gb-headline-text">For those with true passion and dedication for the art, watchmaking, like any other art form, is one that can be mastered and professional watchmaking could well be in your future.</p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-f30bd10a gb-headline-text"><em>Watchmaking is an art form, the ultimate hobby for someone with a fascination for horology</em>.</p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-96a9624f gb-headline-text">Watchmaking has a rich history and heritage with watches dating back to early 16th century Europe.  The original Swiss watch was a mechanical timepiece powered by winding a mainspring and time was kept with a rotating balance spring wheel. </p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-319fa289 gb-headline-text">It was not until the 1960’s that the quartz watch was invented and the 1980’s saw the upheaval of the matchmaking industry known as the ‘quartz crisis’.  Now, in the 21st century, the vast majority of watches on the market are powered by electricity.</p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-e0c89049 gb-headline-text">The <strong><a href="https://watchmakingtools.com/best-watch-case-material/" data-type="post" data-id="10593" data-lasso-id="12394">evolution of watchmaking materials</a></strong> over the years has seen a revolution in the materials used for crafting timepieces. From traditional brass and steel to advanced ceramics and carbon composites, the industry has embraced new technologies to enhance durability and aesthetic appeal.  These materials not only offer improved resistance to wear and tear but also allow for creative design possibilities.  Aspiring watchmakers can explore our guides on material properties and their impact on watchmaking techniques, ensuring their creations stand the test of time.</p>

</div>

<div class="gb-container gb-container-98418b17">

<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-4834b403 gb-headline-text">In the modern world, we have access to an impressive selection of fine watches like <strong><a href="https://watchmakingtools.com/movements/rolex/" data-type="page" data-id="1685" data-lasso-id="12405">Rolex</a></strong>, <strong><a href="https://watchmakingtools.com/movements/omega/" data-type="page" data-id="1611" data-lasso-id="12406">Omega</a>,</strong> and Patek Philippe that can simply be bought off the shelf and even, next day delivered.  However, building and repairing your own watch is a truly rewarding process, one of technological intelligence and fine craftsmanship.  </p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-35a74193 gb-headline-text">Throughout history, horologists were some of the finest craftsmen, and whilst watches are now typically factory manufactured, traditional watchmaking is an excellent way to keep the tradition alive.</p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-83f3dda0 gb-headline-text">Through your journey, you will gain an educated respect for the watchmaking process and the craftsmen of a bygone era. Technological advancements in the world of watchmaking continue to be made and it is a truly fascinating journey to be on.</p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-84746fd1 gb-headline-text"><em>Expand your passion with the help of our excellent resources, incredible guides, and honest reviews to assist you on your watchmaking journey.</em></p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-7e1d2aaf gb-headline-text">Watchmaking is one of the most unique hobbies, great for intellectual stimulation and technological understanding.  It can, however, also be one of complexity and intricacy, a hobby where you will encounter challenges and have to explore how to overcome the issue.</p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-59d2b626 gb-headline-text">Every individual watchmaking journey will be different but there is no doubt that at many corners, you will encounter hurdles and obstacles.  </p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-6d2bde0a gb-headline-text">It is essential that you have great resources to assist you on your watchmaking journey and if you are here at WatchmakingTools, you are already in the right place. From a crucial list of <strong><a href="https://watchmakingtools.com/watchmaking-resources/watch-terminology/" data-type="page" data-id="6234" data-lasso-id="12407">terminology</a></strong> to an up-to-date list of <strong><a href="https://watchmakingtools.com/watchmaking-resources/watch-movement-lift-angles/" data-lasso-id="12408">lift angles</a></strong>, and <strong><a href="https://watchmakingtools.com/watchmaking-resources/watch-movement-hand-sizes/" data-lasso-id="12409">movement hand sizes</a></strong> to our own <a href="https://watchmakingtools.com/watchmaking-resources/watch-batteries/" data-lasso-id="12410"><strong>battery guide</strong></a>, here you can find the basics of how watches work to allow you to start working on your first watch.</p>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-889c8b4f gb-headline-text">Once you have dipped your toe into the wonderful world of timekeeping, expand your passion with the help of our excellent resources, incredible guides, and honest reviews to assist you on your watchmaking journey.</p>
